<userid>109614450247068327429</userid><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMnRfs4GRT8rlZbr6zWJ7X1KKv1OT4UzjDkvty2=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures><rate>5<//rate><date>1526925570385<//date>< Review>
To an outsider, the ice cream scene in LA is competitive with every shop having some sort of novelty flavor to help fight tooth and nail. Most of them are great experiments, but some fly too close to the sun and cause trash cans full of half-eaten cups of disappointment.  COOLHAUS has a bunch of crazy flavors, but the craziest is possibly "milkshake and fries" - an attempt to replicate that feeling of a salty french fry hitting a Wendy's frostee. Against all odds, it's PERFECT. Even the skeptical in my group that never dipped their fries, were won over by this flavor. A perfect blend of malty chocolate and shoestring fries that retain their flavor and firmness (no soggy or frozen potato mouth feel), this is a flavor that'll be every grocery store in the next two years. Eat it here first!</Review>

Ingenious?   Perhaps not.  Nonetheless, these are quite decadent treats.  I would not even like to think about how many grams of sugar are in these build-your-own ice cream sandwiches.

In an earlier review someone mentioned that they were a good deal at $5.  Well, not exactly.  You see, if you really want to build-your-own ice cream sandwiches, this is what you do: 1) Go to your local supermarket, buy a box of their baked-in-house cookies for around $2.50/$5.00; buy a half/gallon of your favorite ice cream around $4.00 and 2) gather your friends, and 3) make an afternoon/evening out of it.</Review>

< Text>
GREAT FOOD & SERVICE! My wife and I were heading back home to Solana beach after visiting her Mom nearby. We Googled food and thankfully a Habit Burger Grill came up about a mile away.The place was very busy when we walked in the front door around 1.30pm but very quickly it was our turn. I even had a quick chat with one of the managers named Brittany while waiting in line. Another manager named Dave served us very efficiently at the cashier desk when we ordered a Teriyaki Charburger and a Tri-Tip Steak Sandwich on sourdough with Teriyaki Sauce.We found a booth table at the rear of the eatery and very soon our food pager went off.Our lunch tasted very fresh, full of quality ingredients, very well presented & most of all...delicious! It was very relaxing to sit in a pristine store and enjoy a very nice lunch before recommencing our long drive home.</Text>
